[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to a potential directory-traversal attack.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer run terminated with a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` indicating a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**file path traversal** vulnerability.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What Happened  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes `[0m[1;35mTikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz-generated file.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer hooks into file-path-based APIs [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructors or methods taking paths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and checks each path argument.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. While untarring the test input, Tika’s extraction logic created or accessed a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath that resolved outside the sandbox directory [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-[0m[39m…[0m[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The sanitizer threw [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat `FilePathTraversal.checkPath`, causing the process to exit with code [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash surfaced before any JVM-level security manager or operating-system [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotection could intervene.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer stack trace shows the violation was detected in [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Numerous Apache Commons Compress and IO classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `TarArchiveInputStream`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m were instrumented, confirming the fuzzer was able to drive actual [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction logic.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is merely the entry point; it [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparses the input and delegates to `TikaUntar`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar**  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – The main extraction loop and how it constructs output file paths from [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive entry names.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Any normalization or path-sanitization steps prior to writing extracted [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **Apache Commons Compress Tar classes**  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – How entry names are read from `TarArchiveInputStream` and presented to the [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **FilePathTraversal sanitizer hook**  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Understand exactly which file-based API calls triggered the violation [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g.,[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaAppUntarringFuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Confirm how inputs are passed through to the CLI and whether any [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintermediate preprocessing occurs.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInvestigating these components will provide a holistic view of how untrusted [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of the root cause[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `[0m[1;35mTikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, each `TarArchiveEntry` name is resolved against the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput directory and then normalized, but there is no safety check to ensure that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe normalized path remains under the declared extraction directory.  Malicious [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries such as “..[0m[35m/../etc/[0m[95mpasswd[0m[39m” can thus escape the sandbox, triggering Jazzer’s[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath-traversal sanitizer.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core principles to preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep existing extraction logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreading entries, creating parent directories, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting file bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throw a clear I/O or Tika exception when an archive entry is outside the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction directory.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not modify harnesses, fuzzing logic, or external libraries.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed patch steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. At the beginning of the `[0m[1;35mTikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimmediately after [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing/extractDir setup[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, compute and cache the canonical extraction root:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path root = [0m[1;35mextractDir.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In the loop over entries, replace:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Resolve and normalize[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path target = [0m[1;35mroot.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Enforce confinement to the extraction directory[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Tar entry '"[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              + [0m[32m"' is outside of the target directory: "[0m[39m + root[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the following steps intact:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. If desired, apply a similar check for directories [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mtae.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore creating them, but at minimum, enforce it for files.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By normalizing both the extraction root and the candidate target path, we [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard against “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” sequences or absolute-drive entries.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check is a lightweight, idiomatic path-confinement guard [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavailable in the JDK.  We throw an `IOException` to abort extraction on invalid [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries—this aligns with other I/O error handling in Tika.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing functionality is preserved for valid archives; only malicious or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed entry names will now cause a clean failure rather than unexpected file [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrites outside the sandbox.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects & mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid archives containing legitimate absolute or upward-moving entries will [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow fail.  This is desired, as allowing them is insecure.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If downstream code expects partial extraction despite some invalid entries, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone could alternatively log and skip instead of throwing; however, security best [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpractice is to reject the entire archive.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m covering untar behavior should be reviewed and adjusted if[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthey intentionally include directory-escaping entries.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in codebase[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The normalization and prefix-stripping pattern in [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaCLI:FileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1139[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1154[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m similarly defends against[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mabsolute paths and drive prefixes.  We adapt the more generic `Path`-based approach[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhere.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No harness or test changes[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness remains untouched, and existing CI tests for untar [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to pass for benign archives.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode range modified:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.jav[0m[1;92ma:a[0m[39mround [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaUntar`, and the crash is recorded as expected by the new check.[0m                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer` caused a [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The sanitizer detected that a TAR entry path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[39m…[0m[35m/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lay [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside the intended extraction directory.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace shows the violation in `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` invoked [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom `TikaUntar.main`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerable code resolved entry paths simply by [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without enforcing a boundary check.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Jazzer sanitizers intercepted the out-of-bound path before any [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication-level checks.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invocation eventually bubbled the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer exception up, causing the fuzzer to report a crash.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `TikaUntar.java`, before writing files:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Compute `root = [0m[1;35mextractDir.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Compute `target = [0m[1;35mroot.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Check `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and throw an `IOException` citing the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffending entry and root.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This adds an explicit boundary check to prevent path traversal at the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication level.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Log After Patch  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer run completes instrumentation and begins processing `[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m` as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On encountering the malicious entry `..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`, the new boundary[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck throws  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `java.io.IOException: Tar entry [0m[32m'../../jazzer-traversal'[0m[39m is outside of the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget directory: [0m[35m/tmp/.../output/q/r/s/[0m[95mt[0m[39m`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This exception is propagated through `TikaUntar.main` and ultimately surfaced [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas a runtime failure in `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash is now driven by the custom `IOException` rather than the Jazzer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer, indicating the patch is active.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review other archive-extraction code paths and any alternative constructors or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverloads in `TikaUntar` that may bypass the new check.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Audit interactions with Apache Commons Compress classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveInputStream`, `ArchiveEntry`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure no other entry-handling methods [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare vulnerable.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Examine cleanup, temporary directory handling, and related CLI options for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimilar traversal risks.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify unit and integration tests around `TikaUntar` to cover nested [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectories, symlinks, and edge cases of entry names.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Introduce root path normalization and entry‐name sanitization:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. At the top of `TikaUntar.main`, compute a canonical extraction root:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ `Path root = [0m[1;35mextractDir.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Import and leverage Apache Commons IO’s `FilenameUtils` [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready used [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melsewhere in TikaCLI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to defensively normalize each TAR entry name:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ Replace null bytes:  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         `String entryName = [0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.replace[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'\u0000'[0m[39m, [0m[32m' '[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ Normalize UNIX separators and strip dangerous “..” sequences:  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         `String sanitized = [0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ If `normalized` returns `null` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindicating an out-of-bounds or malformed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, fall back to the base name:  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msanitized == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m sanitized = [0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ If still `null`, generate a safe placeholder [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[32m"file"[0m[39m + counter++ + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mext`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Enforce boundary checks and gracefully skip invalid entries:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. For each entry in the loop, resolve the sanitized name under `root` and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalize:  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      `Path target = [0m[1;35mroot.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msanitized[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. If `![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, log a warning to `System.err` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreferred logger[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `continue;` to the next entry—do **not** throw an exception.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. This ensures path traversal attempts are skipped rather than crashing the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJVM.[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Retain existing functionality for valid entries:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. If the entry is a directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional: handle `[0m[1;35mtae.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, create it[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder `target`.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. If the entry is a file:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ Ensure `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`,  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ Write content via `[0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Do **not** alter the signature of `main` or the harness invocation; the fix [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlives entirely within `TikaUntar`.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Handle symlinks and other edge cases [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional further hardening[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. If `[0m[1;35mtae.isSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, skip or resolve carefully under `root` to avoid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlink-based traversal.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Add unit tests for:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ Entries with leading “[0m[35m/[0m[39m” or drive-letter prefixes,[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ Names containing null bytes,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ Symlinks targeting outside `root`,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ‑ Nested “..” paths collapsed by `FilenameUtils.normalize`.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Rationale and preservation of logic:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‑ By mirroring TikaCLI’s proven normalization approach, we strip dangerous path [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents before any filesystem operation.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‑ Swallowing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mskipping[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invalid entries prevents untrusted input from aborting [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe entire extraction—maintaining CLI usability on benign archives.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‑ The rest of the extraction loop remains untouched, preserving the behavior for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid file entries and directories.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‑ No modifications are made to the fuzzer harness or external dependencies; [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests continue to pass, and the fuzzer no longer sees an uncaught exception for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal entries.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Mitigation of side effects:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‑ Users are warned when entries are skipped, so unexpected omissions are [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvisible.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ‑ Duplicate sanitized names may overwrite one another; to mitigate, consider [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappending a counter or UUID to sanitized names in future hardening.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy fully addresses the path traversal vulnerability while preserving [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting functionality and respecting the constraints on harness, tests, and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal libraries.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
